<body lang="EN-US">
<div>
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT&nbsp;1.01</font></b></p>
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Flextronics International Ltd.</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Conflict Minerals Report</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">For the reporting period from January&nbsp;1 to December&nbsp;31, 2014</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1. INTRODUCTION</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Conflict Minerals Report (the &#147;<b>Report</b>&#148;) for Flextronics International Ltd. (the &#147;<b>Company</b>,&#148; &#147;<b>we</b>,&#148; &#147;<b>us</b>&#148; or &#147;<b>our</b>&#148;) is provided in accordance with&nbsp;Rule&nbsp;13p-1 under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (&#147;<b>Rule&nbsp;13p-1</b>&#148;) for the reporting period from January&nbsp;1 to December&nbsp;31, 2014 (the &#147;<b>Reporting Period</b>&#148;). The U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (&#147;<b>SEC</b>&#148;) adopted Rule&nbsp;13p-1 in 2012 to implement reporting and disclosure requirements related to certain minerals as directed by the Dodd-Frank Wall Street Reform and Consumer Protection Act. Rule&nbsp;13p-1 requires the disclosure of certain information by SEC registrants (&#147;<b>Registrants</b>&#148;) that manufacture or contract to manufacture products that use minerals specified in Rule&nbsp;13p-1 that are necessary to the functionality or production of these products (&#147;<b>Necessary Conflict Minerals</b>&#148;). These minerals are columbite-tantalite (coltan), cassiterite, wolframite, gold, and their derivatives, which are limited to tantalum, tin, and tungsten (collectively, the &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Conflict </font>Minerals</b>&#148;). Rule&nbsp;13p-1 identifies certain countries from which Conflict Minerals are sourced as &#147;<b>Covered Countries</b>&#148; and requires Registrants to determine, among other things, whether their Necessary Conflict Minerals originated in any Covered Country and fund &#147;Armed Groups&#148; (as such term is defined in Rule&nbsp;13p-1). Covered Countries are of the Democratic Republic of the Congo (the &#147;<b>DRC</b>&#148;) and countries adjoining the DRC.&nbsp; The reporting requirements of Rule&nbsp;13p-1 apply to Registrants regardless of the geographic origin of Conflict Minerals and whether or not such Necessary Conflict Minerals fund Armed Groups in a Covered Country.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Rule&nbsp;13p-1 requires Registrants to conduct, in good faith, a &#147;reasonable country of origin inquiry,&#148; or &#147;<b>RCOI</b>,&#148; with respect to their Necessary Conflict Minerals. The purpose of the RCOI is to determine whether any of the Registrant&#146;s Necessary Conflict Minerals originated in a Covered Country or are from recycled or scrap sources.(1)</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If, based on its RCOI, a Registrant knows that any of its Necessary Conflict Minerals originated in a Covered Country and is not from recycled or scrap sources, or has reason to believe that its Conflict Minerals may have originated in a Covered Country and has reason to believe that its Necessary Conflict Minerals may not be from recycled or scrap sources, the Registrant must exercise due diligence on the source and chain of custody of its&#160; Necessary Conflict Minerals, in accordance with a nationally or internationally recognized due diligence framework, if such a framework is available for the particular Conflict Mineral.&nbsp; Rule&nbsp;13p-1 describes further actions a Registrant must take based on the results of its due diligence on the source and chain of custody of its Conflict Minerals.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We design, build, ship and service complete packaged electronic products to original equipment manufacturers (&#147;<b>OEMs</b>&#148;). We manufacture, or contract to manufacture, many products that use Necessary Conflict Minerals. As primarily a purchaser of component parts, we generally do not purchase raw ore or unrefined Conflict Minerals and do not have direct contractual relationships with the originating mines or smelters of the Conflict Minerals that end up in our products. These mines are many layers upstream from us in our global supply chain, and therefore we need to rely on our thousands of direct suppliers as well as industry initiatives for source information on the Conflict Minerals in our products. In addition, many of our customers require us to use their chosen suppliers in the manufacture of their products and we do not have direct contractual relationships with these suppliers. In such cases</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&nbsp; Rule&nbsp;13p-1 deems that Necessary Conflict Minerals found to originate solely from recycled or scrap services do not fund Armed Groups in any Covered Country.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\105590\15-13049-1\task7434507\13049-1-km-01.htm',USER='105590',CD='May 29 11:46 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">we must rely on the cooperation of our customers and their designated suppliers for Conflict Minerals source information.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In Accordance with the OECD Due Diligence Guidance for Responsible Supply Chains of Minerals from Conflict-Affected and High-Risk Areas (the &#147;<b>OECD Guidance</b>&#148;), the internationally recognized standard on which our company&#146;s Conflict Mineral Compliance system is based, we support an industry initiative that audits smelters&#146; and refiners&#146; due diligence activities. That industry initiative is the Electronic Industry Citizenship Coalition&#146;s (&#147;<b>EICC&#148;</b>) and Global e-Sustainability Initiative&#146;s (&#147;<b>GeSI</b>&#148;) Conflict-Free Sourcing Initiative (&#147;<b>CFSI</b>&#148;). The data on which we relied for certain statements in this report was obtained through our membership in the CFSI, using the Reasonable Country of Origin Inquiry (&#147;<b>RCOI</b>&#148;) report for member &#147;FLEX.&#148; We are a full member of EICC and hold a Board seat in the organization, and are also a member of the CFSI. We embrace and support the CFSI&#146;s due diligence and reporting process to encourage transparency throughout the supply chain.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2. RCOI PROCESS AND RESULTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For products manufactured during the reporting period from January&nbsp;1 to December&nbsp;31, 2014, we performed an RCOI on our Necessary Conflict Minerals. We utilized the CFSI&#146;s Conflict Minerals Reporting Template (&#147;<b>CMRT</b>&#148;) to query the suppliers identified in the assessment of our supply chain as to the sources of the Necessary Conflict Minerals in the products they supply to us. After collecting responses to our CMRT queries from suppliers, we evaluated the responses for completeness and plausibility, and we engaged in follow-up communications with suppliers as appropriate. Some suppliers provided us with &#147;company-level&#148; CMRT responses that include Conflict Mineral information for all products sold by the supplier to its customers even though we may have purchased only a limited subset of such products from the supplier.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on our RCOI described above, we have reason to believe that some of these Conflict Minerals may have originated in DRC or the Covered Countries, and may not be from recycled or scrap sources.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3. DUE DILIGENCE PROCESS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on the results of our RCOI, and as required by Rule&nbsp;13p-1, we conducted due diligence on the source and chain of custody of our Necessary Conflict Minerals to ascertain whether these Conflict Minerals originated in the Covered Countries and financed or benefited Armed Groups in any of these countries.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.1 Design of Our Due Diligence Measures</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As described in Section&nbsp;1 above, the design of our Conflict Minerals due diligence measures conforms with the OECD Guidance, as applicable for tin, tantalum, tungsten, gold and downstream companies (as the term is defined in the OECD Guidance), in all material respects. The design of our due diligence measures followed the following five-step framework as outlined in the OECD Guidance:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Establish strong company management systems.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Identify and assess risks in the supply chain.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Design and implement a strategy to respond to identified risks.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Carry out independent third-party audit of smelters&#146;/refiners&#146; due diligence practices.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Report annually on supply chain due diligence.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2<a name="PB_2_114517_2897"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\105590\15-13049-1\task7434507\13049-1-km-01.htm',USER='105590',CD='May 29 11:46 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.2 Due Diligence Measures Performed</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our implementation of the OECD Guidance comprised the following actions applicable to products manufactured during the reporting period:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of a Conflict Minerals Policy, as further described below;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Creation of a Conflict Minerals Working Group with cross functional team members and executives containing representatives from compliance, corporate social and environmental responsibility, procurement, internal audit and legal;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development of a compliance management framework and implementation plan, including business processes and IT systems to manage information requests and data sharing with customers and suppliers;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Ongoing engagement with customers and suppliers; and</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participation in industry group initiatives to help define and clarify industry standards.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition, we communicated our Conflict Minerals Policy to our suppliers who supply us components containing Conflict Minerals. Our Conflict Minerals Policy includes the following:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our expectation that our suppliers source from socially responsible suppliers;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our expectation that our suppliers have policies and procedures in place to ensure that products and parts supplied to us are &#147;DRC Conflict-free&#148; (as such term is defined in Rule&nbsp;13p-1);</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our expectation that our suppliers provide all necessary due diligence information to confirm that all Conflict Minerals supplied to us are DRC Conflict-free;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our expectation that our suppliers pass these requirements on to their supply chain; and</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The above requirements are taken into consideration when selecting and retaining suppliers.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A copy of our conflict minerals policy was publicly available on our website at http://www.flextronics.com/supplier/supplierquality/default.aspx.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We surveyed 5,601 suppliers of components containing Conflict Minerals, representing approximately 83% of our global direct materials spend for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2014. As with our RCOI, we used the CMRT to collect information from these suppliers regarding the sources of the Necessary Conflict Minerals they supply to us, including the processing smelters or refiners (&#147;<b>SORs</b>&#148;) and countries and mines of origin of such Conflict Minerals.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Of the 5,601 suppliers surveyed, we received responses from 2,756 suppliers. We evaluated the responses for plausibility, consistency and completeness, especially in terms of the reported Conflict Minerals content, and the origin of the Conflict Minerals. We also checked the conflict-free status of smelters and refiners on the CFSI&#146;s website.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We followed-up with the suppliers surveyed, to the extent possible, on missing and inconsistent information, implausible statements regarding no presence of the Conflict Minerals, incomplete data on the CMRT, responses that did not identify smelters or refiners, responses that indicated a sourcing location without complete supporting information from the supply chain, and organizations that were identified as smelters or refiners, but not verified as such through further analysis and research.&nbsp; In addition, we followed-up on cases where a supplier stated that a SOR does not source Necessary Conflict Materials from the Covered Countries, but the reported sourcing country is not a known reserve for the given Conflict Mineral.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If a supplier did not provide the information requested, we initiated an escalation process. The escalation process included contacting alternate persons at the supplier, enlisting help from other Company locations</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3<a name="PB_3_114540_3020"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\JMS\105590\15-13049-1\task7434507\13049-1-km-01.htm',USER='105590',CD='May 29 11:46 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">engaged with the supplier, obtaining assistance from our global commodity team, and working with our customer(s)&nbsp;to contact suppliers.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Following our supplier survey, follow-up and, if necessary, escalation procedures as described above, we estimate we had reliable responses from 2,204 suppliers, representing approximately 57% of our global direct materials spend for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2014, which we used to make our due diligence determination as required under Rule&nbsp;13p-1.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We engaged a third party to assist us with the collection and review of supplier data. For some suppliers, the above activities were completed by the third party on our behalf.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Finally, we periodically report to the Audit Committee of the Company&#146;s Board of Directors with respect to our due diligence process and compliance obligations and will obtain an Independent Private Sector Audit of diligence practices at the appropriate future time as required under Rule&nbsp;13p-1.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4. DUE DILIGENCE DETERMINATION</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on the due diligence performed on the source and chain of custody of the Necessary Conflict Minerals in certain of our products offered in our business groups as described below, we determined that such products are &#147;DRC conflict undeterminable.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4.1 DRC Conflict Undeterminable Products</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">DRC conflict undeterminable products are those for which we were unable to determine whether the Necessary Conflict Minerals contained in such products (not including Conflict Minerals that originate from recycled or scrap sources) directly or indirectly finance or otherwise benefit Armed Groups in the Covered Countries.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.1.1&nbsp;<u>Product Descriptions</u></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We are a globally-recognized leading provider of supply chain solutions that span from concept through consumption.&#160; We design, build, ship, and service complete packaged electronic products for OEMs in the following business groups:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Integrated Network Solutions, which includes radio access base stations, remote radio heads and small cells for wireless infrastructure, optical, routing, broadcasting and switching products for the data and video network, server and storage platforms for both enterprise and cloud based deployments, next generation storage and security appliance products and rack level solutions, converged infrastructure, and software defined product solutions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Consumer Technology Group, which includes our mobile devices business, including smart phones; our consumer electronics business, including connected living, wearable electronics, game consoles, and connectivity devices; and our high-volume computing business, including various supply chain solutions for notebook personal computing, tablets, and printers;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Industrial and Emerging Industries , which is comprised of our semiconductor and capital equipment, office solutions, test and measurement, household industrial and lifestyle, industrial automation and kiosks, energy and metering, and lighting; and</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">High Reliability Solutions, which is comprised of our medical business including medical equipment, disposables, drug delivery, and diagnostics; our automotive business including automotive</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_114603_7748"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\105590\15-13049-1\task7434507\13049-1-km-01.htm',USER='105590',CD='May 29 11:46 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">electronics, automotive lighting, and power electronics, and our defense and aerospace businesses focused on defense, civil aviation, and homeland security;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.1.2&nbsp;<u>Smelters or Refiners; Countries of Origin of Minerals</u></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As noted above, as part of the due diligence process we received and validated declarations on Minerals from 2,204 of our suppliers.&nbsp; These declarations list a total of approximately 161 smelters and 112 refiners. Among the 273 SORs listed in the declarations we received from our suppliers, approximately 73.2% either have been certified as compliant with the Conflict-Free Smelter Program (&#147;<b>CFSP</b>&#148;) assessment protocols or have committed to undergo a CFSP audit.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As many of these declarations are company-wide and not product specific, we believe these declarations may include SORs, and their countries of origin, that do not provide the materials that are used in our products. Due to the many company-wide declarations and the multiple levels of suppliers in our supply chain we are unable to determine with certainty at this time which SORs or which countries of origin listed in the declarations actually provide the specific Conflict Minerals used in our products. The SORs identified by our suppliers in their declarations, as well as their countries of origin, are set forth in the Appendix to this Report.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.1.3&nbsp;<u>Due Diligence Improvement Efforts</u></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We expect to take&nbsp;the following steps, among others, to improve our due diligence processes next year and further mitigate the risk that our Conflict Minerals finance or otherwise benefit Armed Groups in the Covered Countries:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increase supplier outreach as well as the number and quality of supplier survey responses;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Improve quality check of and follow-up process on suppliers&#146; survey responses;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Inform and encourage smelters and refiners to participate in conflict-free industry initiatives and to transition to smelters and refiners identified as conflict free by independent audit programs such as the CFSI;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Actively participate in and support industry trade groups to help bolster awareness and communication throughout the supply chain;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Train and educate our suppliers on our ongoing expectations regarding conflict-free sourcing;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reconsider our partnership with suppliers who do not comply with our Conflict Minerals Policy; and</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Continuing to refine our due diligence processes in accordance with the OECD Guidelines and supplements.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_114617_141"></a></font></p>
